from m_project_general_details pgd
inner join t_project_building_details bd on pgd.Project_Id =bd.Project_Id
inner join t_project_building_wings_details bwd on bd.Project_Building_Id =bwd.Project_Building_Id

from t_project_building_wings_floor_unit_details
where Project_Id =30 and Is_Active=1

select Project_Building_Wings_Id, count(*) as total_unit_count,
sum(case when Is_Residential='Residential' then 1 else 0 end) as residential_unit_count,
sum(case when Is_Residential='Non-Residential' then 1 else 0 end) as non_residential_unit_count
from t_project_building_wings_floor_unit_details
where Project_Id =30 and Is_Active=1
group by Project_Building_Wings_Id
) as t1 on bwd.Project_Building_Wings_Id =t1.Project_Building_Wings_Id
where bwd.Project_Id = 30 and bwd.Is_Active=1

from t_project_building_wings_floor_unit_details
